cat_col='category_id'):\n    d=df.copy().merge(users[['user_id','city','user_type']], left_on=user_col, right_on='user_id', how='inner')\n    if listing_join:\n        d=d.merge(listings[['listing_id','category_name']], on='listing_id')\n    else:\n        d=d.merge(cat[['category_id','category_name']], left_on=cat_col, right_on='category_id')\n tc_share=d.groupby(['user_type','category_name']).size().rename('tc').reset_index()\n    t_total=d.groupby('user_type').size().rename('type_total').reset_index()\n    tc_share=tc_share.merge(t_total,on='user_type')\n    tc_share['share']=tc_share['tc']/tc_share['type_total']\n    exp=ct_total.merge(tc_share[['user_type','category_name','share']], on='user_type')\n    exp['expected']=exp['city_type_total']*exp['share']\n    exp=exp.groupby(['city','category_name'])['expected'].sum().reset_index()\n    full=pd.MultiIndex.from_product([major_cities, leaf], names=['city','category_name']).to_frame(index=False)\n    full=full.merge(obs, on=['city','category_name'], how='left').merge(exp, on=['city','category_name'], how='left').fillna(0)\n    full['z']=(full['obs']-full['expected'])/np.sqrt(full['expected'].where(full['expected']>0,np.nan))\n    return full[['city','category_name','obs','expected','z']]\nsearches=pd.concat([pd.read_csv(f, ignore_index=True)\ncat=pd.read_csv(base/'category_001.csv', cat_col='category_id'):\n    d=df.copy().merge(users[['user_id','city','user_type']], left_on=user_col, right_on='user_id', how='inner')\n    if listing_join:\n        d=d.merge(listings[['listing_id','category_name']], on='listing_id')\n    else:\n        d=d.merge(cat[['category_id','category_name']], left_on=cat_col, right_on='category_id')\n    obs=d.groupby(['city','category_name']).size().rename('obs').reset_index()\n    ct_total=d.groupby(['city','user_type']).size().rename('city_type_total').reset_index()\n    tc_share=d.groupby(['user_type','category_name']).size().rename('tc').reset_index()\n    t_total=d.groupby('user_type').size().rename('type_total').reset_index()\n    tc_share=tc_share.merge(t_total,on='user_type')\n    tc_share['share']=tc_share['tc']/tc_share['type_total']\n    exp=ct_total.merge(tc_share[['user_type','category_name','share']], on='user_type')\n    exp['expected']=exp['city_type_total']*exp['share']\n    exp=exp.groupby(['city','category_name'])['expected'].sum().reset_index()\n    full=pd.MultiIndex.from_product([major_cities, leaf], names=['city','category_name']).to_frame(index=False)\n    full=full.merge(obs, on=['city','category_name'], how='left').merge(exp, on=['city','category_name'], how='left').fillna(0)\n    full['z']=(full['obs']-full['expected'])/np.sqrt(full['expected'].where(full['expected']>0,np.nan))\n    return full[['city','category_name','z']]\nsearches=pd.concat([pd.read_csv(f, usecols=['user_id','category_id']) for f in sorted(base.glob('search_event_*.csv'))], ignore_index=True)\nclicks=pd.concat([pd.read_csv(f, usecols=['user_id','listing_id']) for f in sorted(base.glob('click_event_*.csv'))], ignore_index=True)\nfav=pd.read_csv(base/'favorite_event_001.csv', usecols=['user_id','listing_id'])\npur=pd.read_csv(base/'purchase_001.csv', usecols=['buyer_id','listing_id'])\nrs=residuals(searches,'user_id',False,'category_id').rename(columns={'z':'search_z'})\nrc=residuals(clicks,'user_id',True).rename(columns={'z':'click_z'})\nrf=residuals(fav,'user_id',True).rename(columns={'z':'fav_z'})\nrp=residuals(pur,'buyer_id',True).rename(columns={'z':'pur_z'})\nfull=rs.merge(rc,on=['city','category_name']).merge(rf,on=['city','category_name']).merge(rp,on=['city','category_name'])\nfull['combined4']=full[['search_z','click_z','fav_z','pur_z']].mean(axis=1)\nfor
